name:Aâ€nâ€oâ€nâ€yâ€mâ€oâ€uâ€sâ€ â€Uâ€sâ€eâ€r
info:Comfy Queen Room
info:Stayed in January 2024
info:Family
info:28 Reviews
rating:3.5
posted:Posted February 5, 2024
msg:The environment of the hotel is quite good, the room is also very large, and I am very satisfied with the hardware facilities. There were few people staying that day in the off-season, so I was upgraded.
But the service felt bad. Breakfast was served at 7 o'clock, but it was not ready when I went there at 7:10, and the pots for hot dishes were empty. It was finally almost full at 7:30. There were two steamed fish in total. The aunt in charge of breakfast took away most of them with a stainless steel basin, leaving only a few pieces of meat and the head and tail. Before we started to take the remaining dishes, he took them away first. This happened for two days. After breakfast, I also reported to the front desk about the problem that the food was not ready at breakfast time, but the front desk said nothing.
On the second day, the bathroom sewer was blocked and the water flooded to the floor of the bathroom. I called the front desk, and the aunt who came to clean it up only solved the problem of sewer blockage and did not care about the water on the ground. We called her back again, and she said that there was only a wet mop, and finally we used the bath towel in our room to wipe the ground.
In general, it was not like the service that a five-star hotel should have. It was like a small family workshop, and the management was not good.
